 3
 It is better that you buy the required items for the whole month before the month of Ramadan starts, so that you do not have to wander outside in the condition of fasting and you can spend more time in prayer
 4

 11

 12

 13

 14

 However, Union Minister Alphons Kannanthanam has said that the Disaster Management Act 2005 does not have a provision to declare a disaster as a national disaster
 aaie jaanate hai ki rashtriya aapadaa orgambhir aapadaamen kya antar hota he
 Definition of Disaster According to the Disaster Management Act, 2005, 'disaster' means any catastrophe, destruction, destruction, etc
 caused by natural or anthropogenic reasons in any area, or due to accident or neglect, which results in huge loss of human life or property
 Causing heavy damage and destruction, or extensive damage to the environment and to be so large that it is not possible for the local community to deal with
 prakritik or maanav janit aapadabukamp, baadh, bhuskhalan, chakravaat, tsunami, shahari ilaakon main baadh, lu aadi ko 'prakritik aapadaa' mana jaataa he, jabaki newclear, biological or chemical aapadaaon ko 'maanav janit aapadaa' mana jaataa he
 How to decide National disaster: There is no government or legal provision to consider any disaster as a national disaster
 haal hi main sansad ke monsoon satr main grih rajya mantri kiran rigiju ne kaha tha, 'state dizaster respance fund (SDRF) yaa neshnal dizaster respance fund (NDRF) kii maujuuda guideline iske bare main nahin bataati ki kis aapadaa ko 'rashtriya aapadaa' ghoshit kiya jaae
 'the answer to many questions is not decided
 The proposal came up for consideration before the Fifth Finance Commission (1995-2000) that a disaster can be declared a' national disaster of extraordinary intensity 'if it affects one-third of the state's population
 You do ayog ne ise sweekaar to kiya, lekin yah tay nahin kiya ki 'asaadhaaran prachandta kii aapadaa' kise kahenge
 But the commission said that it would depend on case to case, that is, it can be decided according to individual cases
 uttarakhand main badal fatne se ai baadh or chakravaat hudahud kois tarah kii aapadaghoshit kiya gaya tha
 Which fund in which disaster? According to the National Disaster Management Policy, the state government has to provide relief from the State Disaster Response Fund
 agar gambhir prakruti kii aapadaa hoti he to hi neshnal dizaster rispons fund (andiaref) se madad uplabdh karai jaati he
